1600<h3>

1601Where to Use Tile in Your Home</h3>

1602

1603<p>

1604Thanks to its durability and the pleasing patterns it creates, tile is incredibly versatile. For bathrooms, add tile to the floors, walls, or showers. Change it up and use different tiles for the floor than the wall to create a different look and style.&nbsp;</p>

1605

1606<p>

1607For the kitchen, use porcelain or ceramic tile on the floor for durability and style. Glass tile works well for backsplashes, offering easy cleanup when it comes to dust and grease splashes. Peel and stick tile also works well to add an easy-to-clean backsplash thats easy to install.&nbsp;</p>

1608

1609<p>

1610Add tile to a fireplace or mantel to add decorative elements to turn a functional element of your home into a beautiful statement piece.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p>

1611

1612<p>

1613Have questions about which tile is best for your home? Ask our design experts now by chat, email, or call 1-855-483-2629.</p>
